# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Update playlist based on action #

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun pl, a ->
    case a
    | PlaySong(id) =>
        let (songs, current_song) = pl

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun pl, a ->
    case a
    | PlaySong(id) =>
        let (songs, current_song) = pl in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #

  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# -1 if none is playing #

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun pl, a ->
    case a
    | PlaySong(id) =>
        let (songs, current_song) = pl in
        if id == current_song then (songs, -1) else (songs, id)

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun pl, a ->
    case a
    | PlaySong(id) =>
        let (songs, current_song) = pl in
        if id == current_song then (songs, -1) else (songs, id) end

# Non-negative ID for songs #
type Id = Int in

# Actions user can do in a playlist #
type PlayListAction =
  + PlaySong(Id)
  + PauseCurrentSong
  + RemoveSong(Id)
  + AddSong(Id)
in

# A playlist with a list of songs and the id for the currently playing/paused song #
# -1 if none is playing #
type PlayList = ([Id], Id) in

# Update playlist based on action #
let update: (PlayList, PlayListAction) -> PlayList =
  fun pl, a ->
    case a
    | PlaySong(id) =>
        let (songs, current_song) = pl in
        if id == current_song then (songs, -1) else (songs, id) end
